<p><b>级数</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Series</span>）是<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>中一个有穷或无穷的<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97" title="序列">序列</a>例如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},u_{4}\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>4</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},u_{4}\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},u_{4}\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/43762d8b7dc5bfc3f3d05ac32faf68deb864c9ac" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:15.748ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>之和，即<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle s=u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>s</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle s=u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle s=u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6aef35d06fab2b7a3b1470988e6ff6da3a090b77" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:22.585ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>，如果序列是有穷序列，其和称为有穷级数；反之，称为无穷级数（一般也简称为级数）。
</p><p>序列<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{0},u_{1},u_{2},\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle u_{0},u_{1},u_{2},\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle u_{0},u_{1},u_{2},\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a8511a30c00dddfca2a1f34c32ae4b5d43353a93" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:12.977ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>中的项称作级数的通项（或一般项）。级数的通项可以是<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0" title="实数">实数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%9F%A9%E9%98%B5" title="矩阵">矩阵</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F" title="向量">向量</a>等常量，也可以是关于其他变量的<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="函数">函数</a>，不一定是一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0" title="数">数</a>。一般的，如果级数的通项是常量，则称之为常数项级数，如果级数的通项是函数，则称之为函数项级数。常见的简单有穷数列的级数包括<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E5%B7%AE%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="等差数列">等差数列</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E6%AF%94%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="等比数列">等比数列</a>的级数。
</p><p>有穷数列的级数一般通过<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%9D%E7%AD%89%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0" title="初等代数">初等代数</a>的方法就可以求得。无穷级数有发散和收敛的区别，称为无穷级数的敛散性。判断无穷级数的敛散性是无穷级数研究中的主要工作。无穷级数在收敛时才会有一个和；<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%91%E6%95%A3%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="发散级数">发散的无穷级数</a>在一般意义上没有和，但可以用一些别的方式来定义。
</p><p>无穷级数的研究更多的需要<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="数学分析">数学分析</a>的方法来解决。无穷级数一般写作<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \textstyle u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>+</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \textstyle u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \textstyle u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c997d2c79b2ff3ff70ac5c8af588cd40aa73204d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:18.396ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \textstyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mstyle displaystyle="false" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \textstyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \textstyle \sum u_{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b33e1c2855350ffe7026fc52d93306565adf70d7" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.389ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>或者<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<munderover>
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munderover>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1996a53b9365ee5e345fe7dc1b86df610634e7af" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:6.29ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span>，级数收敛时，其和通常被表示为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle s=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>s</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<munderover>
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munderover>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle s=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle s=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8d3a81b305981fc26f2df5dff934e2253afb8230" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:10.479ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span>，其中符号<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f1d4e06539576633987e902f402ed46728d573b6" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:3.355ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>称为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%82%E5%92%8C%E5%8F%B7" title="求和号">求和号</a>。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无穷级数的定义">无穷级数的定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：无穷级数的定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (u_{n})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (u_{n})}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="(u_{n})" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/551294aa20e8ed2ba0f65099a0b5bf830b9827cb" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.357ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是一个无穷序列 ：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},\ldots ,u_{n},\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
<mo>,</mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},\ldots ,u_{n},\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle u_{1},u_{2},u_{3},\ldots ,u_{n},\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7ca0f21724f625b1ccbbb9a752c9571984228973" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:20.703ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>，其前n项的和称为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>的<b>部分和</b>：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle s_{n}=u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\cdots +u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>s</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>

<h2><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E6.95.9B.E6.95.A3.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无穷级数的敛散性">无穷级数的敛散性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：无穷级数的敛散性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h3><span id=".E4.BB.BB.E6.84.8F.E9.A1.B9.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="任意项级数">任意项级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：任意项级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>如果级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

将<b>任意项级数</b>各项<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }|u_{n}|=|u_{1}|+|u_{2}|+|u_{3}|+\cdots +|u_{n}|+\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E7.BB.9D.E5.AF.B9.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="绝对收敛">绝对收敛</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：绝对收敛">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd>如果级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }|u_{n}|}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>定理：如果任意项级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="收敛级数的性质">收敛级数的性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：收敛级数的性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>若一个无穷级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}\ :\ u_{1}+u_{2}+u_{3}+\cdots +u_{n}+\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<ul><li>收敛的无穷级数可以逐项相加或相减，如有两个无穷级数：</li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }u_{n}=s}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle s=u_{12}+u_{15}+u_{16}+u_{17}+\cdots +u_{n}+\cdots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle s=u_{12}+u_{15}+u_{16}+u_{17}+\cdots +u_{n}+\cdots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2efaae862f7d702f3b441383e8b269412bfef88d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:42.05ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这两个级数的敛散性是一样的。
</p>
<ul><li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>趋向无限大时，任何一个收敛级数的通项都趋于0：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }u_{n}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\lim _{n\to \infty }u_{n}=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c93a30874c887769d0835535ab67fec95916b59d" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:11.469ex; height:3.676ex;"/></span></li></ul>
<ul><li>在一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%A4%87%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="完备空间">完备空间</a>中，也可以运用<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E5%88%A4%E5%88%A5%E6%B3%95" title="柯西判别法">柯西收敛</a>的准则来判断级数是否收敛：一个无穷级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{+\infty }u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle |s_{n}-s_{m}|=|\sum _{k=m+1}^{n}u_{k}|=|u_{m+1}+u_{m+2}+\cdots +u_{n}|&lt;\epsilon }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/dc4ad6b1b8a04c5b5afcae526ca25e3357d300b9" style="vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:54.909ex; height:7.009ex;"/></span>。</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6.E5.8E.86.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="无穷级数的研究历史">无穷级数的研究历史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：无穷级数的研究历史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>将一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="函数">函数</a>展开成无穷级数的概念最早来自14世纪<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%B0%E5%BA%A6" title="印度">印度</a>的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A9%AC%E5%BE%B7%E5%93%88%E7%93%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="马德哈瓦（页面不存在）">马德哈瓦</a>。他首先发展了<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="幂级数">幂级数</a>的概念，对<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="泰勒级数">泰勒级数</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%BA%A6%E5%85%8B%E5%8A%B3%E6%9E%97%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="麦克劳林级数">麦克劳林级数</a>、无穷级数的有理逼近以及无穷<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E5%88%86%E6%95%B0" title="连分数">连分数</a>做了研究。他发现了<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6" title="正弦">正弦</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BD%99%E5%BC%A6" title="余弦">余弦</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%88%87" title="正切">正切函数</a>等的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="泰勒级数">泰勒展开</a>，还用幂级数计算了 <b><a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%93%E5%91%A8%E7%8E%87" title="圆周率">π</a></b> 的值。他的学生继承和发展了他关于级数的工作。
</p><p>17世纪，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A9%B9%E5%A7%86%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%A0%BC%E9%87%8C%E9%AB%98%E5%88%A9" title="詹姆斯·格里高利">詹姆斯·格里高利</a>也开始研究无穷级数，并发表了若干函数的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="泰勒级数">麦克劳林展开</a>式。1715年，<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%83%E9%B2%81%E5%85%8B%C2%B7%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92" title="布鲁克·泰勒">布鲁克·泰勒</a>提出了构造一般解析函数的泰勒级数的方法。18世纪时<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>又发展了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="超几何级数">超几何级数</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Q-%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Q-级数（页面不存在）">q-级数</a>的理论。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AF.B9.E5.AE.A1.E6.95.9B.E6.B3.95.E7.9A.84.E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="对审敛法的研究">对审敛法的研究</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：对审敛法的研究">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>14世纪时，<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A9%AC%E5%BE%B7%E5%93%88%E7%93%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="马德哈瓦（页面不存在）">马德哈瓦</a>已经开始讨论判别无穷级数敛散性的方法。他提出了一些审敛的准则，后来他的学生将其推广。
</p><p>然而在<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%B4%B2" title="欧洲">欧洲</a>，审查无穷级数是否收敛的研究一般被认为是从19世纪由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="高斯">高斯</a>开始的。他于1812年发表了关于<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>的超几何级数
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1+{\frac {\alpha \beta }{1\cdot \gamma }}x+{\frac {\alpha (\alpha +1)\beta (\beta +1)}{1\cdot 2\cdot \gamma (\gamma +1)}}x^{2}+\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<mi>α<!-- α --></mi>
<mi>β<!-- β --></mi>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>⋅<!-- ⋅ --></mo>
<mi>γ<!-- γ --></mi>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>γ<!-- γ --></mi>
<mo>+</mo>

<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<mo>⋯<!-- ⋯ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1+{\frac {\alpha \beta }{1\cdot \gamma }}x+{\frac {\alpha (\alpha +1)\beta (\beta +1)}{1\cdot 2\cdot \gamma (\gamma +1)}}x^{2}+\cdots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 1+{\frac {\alpha \beta }{1\cdot \gamma }}x+{\frac {\alpha (\alpha +1)\beta (\beta +1)}{1\cdot 2\cdot \gamma (\gamma +1)}}x^{2}+\cdots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/82e1883c70ac468723de21e81145fbd7335b0c69" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:39.16ex; height:6.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>的论文，提出了一些简单的收敛准则，并对余项和以及收敛半径进行了讨论。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF" title="柯西">柯西</a>提出了严格的审敛法的重要性，他证明了两个收敛级数的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E4%B9%98%E7%A7%AF" title="柯西乘积">乘积</a>不一定是收敛的，同时开始研究严格的审敛准则。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89" title="欧拉">欧拉</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%98%E6%96%AF" title="高斯">高斯</a>各自给出了各种审敛法则。柯西更研究了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A4%87%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="复函数">复函数</a>的幂级数展开。
</p><p>1826年，<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94" title="阿贝尔">阿贝尔</a>在他的关于<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%8C%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="二项式级数（页面不存在）">二项式级数</a>
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1+{\frac {m}{1}}x+{\frac {m(m-1)}{2!}}x^{2}+\cdots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mi>m</mi>
<mn>1</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<mi>m</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>m</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>!</mo>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<mo>⋯<!-- ⋯ --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1+{\frac {m}{1}}x+{\frac {m(m-1)}{2!}}x^{2}+\cdots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="1+{\frac {m}{1}}x+{\frac {m(m-1)}{2!}}x^{2}+\cdots " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9ec6fa3146d4c1da1f43866db7b7ab4c3e827c48" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:29.726ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>的论文中更正了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF" title="柯西">柯西</a>的若干个结论，并给出了<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%8C%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="二项式级数（页面不存在）">二项式级数</a>的严格的求和方法，指出了<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD" title="连续">连续性</a>在收敛问题中的重要性。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF" title="柯西">柯西</a>提出的审敛法并不是普遍适用的，只能用于判别某些特定函数的敛散性。同时代的其他数学家，比如拉贝（Joseph Ludwig Raabe）的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="对数判别法（页面不存在）">对数判别法</a>，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E6%91%A9%E6%A0%B9" title="德·摩根">德·摩根</a>的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="对数判别法（页面不存在）">对数判别法</a>（被 DuBois-Reymond和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%99%AE%E6%9E%97%E6%96%AF%E6%B5%B7%E5%A7%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="普林斯海姆（页面不存在）">普林斯海姆</a>证明对某些函数失效）
，以及<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%84%E7%91%9F%C2%B7%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%E8%98%AD" title="约瑟·伯特兰">贝特朗</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%96%AF%E6%89%98%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF" title="斯托克斯">斯托克斯</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%87%E6%AF%94%E9%9B%AA%E5%A4%AB" title="切比雪夫">切比雪夫</a>等人的审敛法也是如此。
</p><p>对普遍的审敛法则的研究由<a href="/wiki/%E6%81%A9%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%C2%B7%E5%BA%93%E9%BB%98%E5%B0%94" title="恩斯特·库默尔">恩斯特·库默尔</a>开始，之后的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E6%A3%AE%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6" title="艾森斯坦">艾森斯坦</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BB%B4%E5%B0%94%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="维尔斯特拉斯">维尔斯特拉斯</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%A4%E9%87%8C%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E8%BF%AA%E5%B0%BC&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尤里斯·迪尼（页面不存在）">尤里斯·迪尼</a>等都曾致力于这一领域。普林斯海姆于1889年发表的论文阐述了完整的普适审敛理论。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AF.B9.E4.B8.80.E8.87.B4.E8.BF.9E.E7.BB.AD.E6.80.A7.E7.9A.84.E7.A0.94.E7.A9.B6"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="对一致连续性的研究">对一致连续性的研究</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：对一致连续性的研究">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>1821年，柯西首先开始对<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD" title="一致连续">一致连续性</a>的研究，但其中有不少错误和局限。这些错误最早被<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94" title="阿贝尔">阿贝尔</a>指出，但首先得出正确结论的是<a href="/wiki/%E8%8F%B2%E5%88%A9%E6%99%AE%C2%B7%E8%B7%AF%E5%BE%B7%E7%BB%B4%E5%B8%8C%C2%B7%E5%86%AF%C2%B7%E8%B5%9B%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%94" title="菲利普·路德维希·冯·赛德尔">西德尔</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%B9%94%E6%B2%BB%C2%B7%E5%8A%A0%E5%B8%83%E9%87%8C%E5%9F%83%C2%B7%E6%96%AF%E6%89%98%E5%85%8B%E6%96%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="乔治·加布里埃·斯托克斯（页面不存在）">斯托克斯</a>。1853年，柯西在注意到阿贝尔的批评后重新开展研究，并得到了与斯托克斯一样的结论。然而，一致连续性的重要性在很长一段时间里没有受到重视。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.B1.BB.E5.88.AB"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="类别">类别</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：类别">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<dl><dd>更多级数请参见<a href="/wiki/%E7%B4%9A%E6%95%B8%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8" title="级数列表">级数列表</a>。</dd></dl>
<h3><span id=".E5.87.A0.E4.BD.95.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="几何级数">几何级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：几何级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E7%B4%9A%E6%95%B8" title="几何级数">几何级数</a></div>
<p><b>几何级数</b>（或<b>等比级数</b>）是指通项为<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%89%E6%AF%94%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="等比数列">等比数列</a>的级数，比如：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1+{1 \over 2}+{1 \over 4}+{1 \over 8}+{1 \over 16}+\cdots =\sum _{n=0}^{\infty }{1 \over 2^{n}}=2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.B0.83.E5.92.8C.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="调和级数">调和级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：调和级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E8%B0%83%E5%92%8C%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="调和级数">调和级数</a></div>
<p><b>调和级数</b>是指通项为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {1 \over n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1+{1 \over 2}+{1 \over 3}+{1 \over 4}+{1 \over 5}+\cdots =\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{1 \over n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".7F.27.22.60UNIQ--postMath-00000048-QINU.60.22.27.7F-.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="'&quot;`UNIQ--postMath-00000048-QINU`&quot;'-级数"><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>-级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title='编辑章节：&lt;span class="mwe-math-element"&gt;&lt;span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"&gt;&lt;math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p}"&gt;

<p><i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span></i>-级数是指通项为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {1}{n^{p}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle U_{p}=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{n^{p}}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</munderover>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<msup>
<mi>n</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</msup>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle U_{p}=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{n^{p}}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="U_{p}=\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }{\frac {1}{n^{p}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ab8f4d7ec6762883730a1dc177ff5b4a3381a096" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:12.777ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>对于实数值的<i><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span></i>，当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
<mo>&gt;</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p&gt;1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p&gt;1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0f127e7a5f2449ddf3edb8164c2d2439120641f9" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:5.52ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>时收敛，当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p\leq 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
<mo>≤<!-- ≤ --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p\leq 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle p\leq 1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6752d6a173f1eac0dba878e0a9bcd6a4016c2e36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:5.52ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>时发散。这可以由<b>积分比较审敛法</b>得出。
</p><p>函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta :p\mapsto U_{p}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ζ<!-- ζ --></mi>
<mo>:</mo>
<mi>p</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">↦<!-- ↦ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>U</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>p</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \zeta :p\mapsto U_{p}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\zeta :p\mapsto U_{p}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f2473dd43d80825fd7823e2decf9ea277d4ddc3e" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:10.462ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%CE%B6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="黎曼ζ函数">黎曼ζ函数</a>在实轴大于1的部分的限制，关于黎曼<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \zeta }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \zeta }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\zeta" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d5c3916703cae7938143d38865f78f27faadd4ae" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.095ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>函数有着名的<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%E7%8C%9C%E6%83%B3" title="黎曼猜想">黎曼猜想</a>。
特别地，当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

</semantics>

<semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/81eac1e205430d1f40810df36a0edffdc367af36" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:1.259ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>-级数即为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%AA%BF%E5%92%8C%E7%B4%9A%E6%95%B8" title="调和级数">调和级数</a>。
</p>

<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=1}^{\infty }(b_{n}-b_{n+1})}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E6.B3.B0.E5.8B.92.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="泰勒级数">泰勒级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：泰勒级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%B0%E5%8B%92%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="泰勒级数">泰勒级数</a></div>
<p><b>泰勒级数</b>是关于一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E6%BB%91" title="光滑">光滑</a>函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>在一点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>附近取值的级数。泰勒函数由函数在点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的各阶导数值构成，具体形式为：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=0}^{\infty }{\frac {f^{(n)}(a)}{n!}}(x-a)^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<munderover>
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munderover>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<msup>
<mi>f</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>!</mo>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum _{n=0}^{\infty }{\frac {f^{(n)}(a)}{n!}}(x-a)^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum _{n=0}^{\infty }{\frac {f^{(n)}(a)}{n!}}(x-a)^{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8c116d3aee442eca69ccfaa86b4ac2f1466ae20" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; width:19.863ex; height:7.176ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>这是一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="幂级数">幂级数</a>。如果它在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>附近收敛，那么就称函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>在点<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>上是解析的。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BA.A4.E9.94.99.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="交错级数">交错级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：交错级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>具有以下形式的级数
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=0}^{\infty }(-1)^{n}a_{n}\!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<munderover>
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munderover>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
<msub>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mspace width="negativethinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum _{n=0}^{\infty }(-1)^{n}a_{n}\!}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum _{n=0}^{\infty }(-1)^{n}a_{n}\!" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8fc27941230015037defff1baf5fa1e6cc91a12" style="vertical-align: -3.005ex; margin-right: -0.387ex; width:11.802ex; height:6.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>其中所有的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/790f9209748c2dca7ed7b81932c37c02af1dbc31" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span><a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9F%E6%95%B0" title="负数">非负</a>，被称作<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E9%94%99%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="交错级数">交错级数</a>。交错级数的收敛通常要借助<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95" title="莱布尼茨判别法">莱布尼茨判别法</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.B9.82.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="幂级数">幂级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：幂级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="幂级数">幂级数</a></div>
<p>形同<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum a_{n}(x-x_{0})^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>a</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
<msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum a_{n}(x-x_{0})^{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum a_{n}(x-x_{0})^{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7388770cb8bad2709d4ae70154722a55a3aed112" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:15.772ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>的函数项无穷级数称为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x-x_{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>0</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x-x_{0}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x-x_{0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/04e662f057bc1d31f195d512e0e96a831fc8afea" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:6.554ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>的<b>幂级数</b>。它的收敛与否和系数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/790f9209748c2dca7ed7b81932c37c02af1dbc31" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>有关。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.82.85.E9.87.8C.E5.8F.B6.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="傅里叶级数">傅里叶级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="编辑章节：傅里叶级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%82%85%E9%87%8C%E5%8F%B6%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="傅里叶级数">傅里叶级数</a></div>
<p>任何<a href="/wiki/%E5%91%A8%E6%9C%9F%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="周期函数">周期函数</a>都可以用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%BC%A6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="正弦函数">正弦函数</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BD%99%E5%BC%A6%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="余弦函数">余弦函数</a>构成的无穷级数来表示，称为<b>傅里叶级数</b>。傅里叶级数是函数项无穷级数，也就是说每项都是一个函数。傅里叶级数在<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E8%AE%BA" title="数论">数论</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%84%E5%90%88%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="组合数学">组合数学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E5%8F%B7%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="信号处理">信号处理</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%A6%82%E7%8E%87%E8%AE%BA" title="概率论">概率论</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%9F%E8%AE%A1%E5%AD%A6" title="统计学">统计学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E7%A0%81%E5%AD%A6" title="密码学">密码学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%A3%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="声学">声学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E5%AD%A6" title="光学">光学</a>等领域都有着广泛的应用。
</p><p>例如，周期为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2\pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)={\frac {a_{0}}{2}}+\sum _{n=1}^{\infty }(a_{n}\cos nx+b_{n}\sin nx),n=1,2,3,\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E5.B8.B8.E6.95.B0.E9.A1.B9.E6.97.A0.E7.A9.B7.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E5.AE.A1.E6.95.9B.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="常数项无穷级数审敛法">常数项无穷级数审敛法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="编辑章节：常数项无穷级数审敛法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%A1%E6%95%9B%E6%B3%95" title="审敛法">审敛法</a></div>
<h3><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E9.A1.B9.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正项级数">正项级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="编辑章节：正项级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>若通项为实数的无穷级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>每一项<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6c7339b0b08d3045d72ddbacf4a3e50d24640c2d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.548ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>都大于等于零，则称<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>是一<b>正项级数</b>。
</p><p>如果无穷级数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span> 是正项级数，则部分和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>S</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9f049ac28d4ac8097b625f9d71c1f22b2ebd1bc4" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.643ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>是一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%96%AE%E8%AA%BF" title="单调">单调</a>递增数列。由数列极限的判别准则：单调<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%95%8C" title="有界">有界</a>数列必有极限。因此，倘若部分和数列<i>S<sub>n</sub></i>有界，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>收敛，且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }S_{n}=s}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<munder>
<mo form="prefix" movablelimits="true">lim</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munder>
<msub>
<mi>S</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>s</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }S_{n}=s}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\lim _{n\to \infty }S_{n}=s" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/730ce9d6ffd380bf8f3277c143bfb1535b1e64bf" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:11.492ex; height:3.676ex;"/></span> ;反之，若部分和数列趋于正无穷，级数发散。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E6.AF.94.E8.BE.83.E5.88.A4.E5.88.AB.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="比较判别法">比较判别法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="编辑章节：比较判别法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span> 同时收敛或发散。</dd></dl>
<p>比如，我们已知级数：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum {1 \over n^{2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</p><p>比较判别法的特点是要已知若干级数的敛散性。一般来说，我们可以选择比较简单的级数：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle U_{p}=\sum {1 \over n^{p}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h4><span id=".E8.BE.BE.E6.9C.97.E8.B4.9D.E5.B0.94.E5.88.A4.E5.88.AB.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="达朗贝尔判别法">达朗贝尔判别法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：达朗贝尔判别法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BE%BE%E6%9C%97%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95" title="达朗贝尔判别法">达朗贝尔审敛法</a></div>
<p>在比较判别法中，如果取几何级数为比较的标准级数，可得：
</p>
<dl><dd>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>

<ul><li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0a281c61029226f478174e5c54032404fa199ab8" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:6.29ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>可能收敛也可能发散。</li></ul></dd></dl>
<p>这个判别法也称为<b>比值判别法</b>或<b>比值审敛法</b>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E6.9F.AF.E8.A5.BF.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E5.87.86.E5.88.99"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="柯西收敛准则">柯西收敛准则</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="编辑章节：柯西收敛准则">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E6%A0%B9%E5%80%BC%E5%AE%A1%E6%95%9B%E6%B3%95" title="根值审敛法">根值审敛法</a></div>
<dl><dd>设 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}</annotation>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<munder>

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">→<!-- → --></mo>
<mi mathvariant="normal">∞<!-- ∞ --></mi>
</mrow>
</munder>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mroot>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</mroot>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>p</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \lim _{n\to \infty }{\sqrt[{n}]{u_{n}}}=p}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\lim _{n\to \infty }{\sqrt[{n}]{u_{n}}}=p" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a680b883b2fadafef4932265aaac629ff3862d93" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:13.412ex; height:3.676ex;"/></span>，则
<ul><li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p&lt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>p</mi>
<mo>&lt;</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p&lt;1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="p&lt;1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f40fda4df30e9f9f3354c808cc122e5dadbc2d99" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:5.52ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>时，级数 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p&gt;1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li>当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle p=1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>这个判别法也称为<b>根值判别法</b>或<b>根值审敛法'</b>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E4.BA.A4.E9.94.99.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="交错级数_2">交错级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="编辑章节：交错级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E9%94%99%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95" title="交错级数判别法">交错级数判别法</a></div>
<p>具有以下形式的级数
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum _{n=0}^{\infty }(-1)^{n}a_{n}\!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<p>其中所有的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a_{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a_{n}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/790f9209748c2dca7ed7b81932c37c02af1dbc31" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span><a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9F%E6%95%B0" title="负数">非负</a>，被称作<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E9%94%99%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="交错级数">交错级数</a>。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E8.8E.B1.E5.B8.83.E5.B0.BC.E8.8C.A8.E5.88.A4.E5.88.AB.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="莱布尼茨判别法">莱布尼茨判别法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="编辑章节：莱布尼茨判别法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%8E%B1%E5%B8%83%E5%B0%BC%E8%8C%A8%E5%88%A4%E5%88%AB%E6%B3%95" title="莱布尼茨判别法">莱布尼茨审敛法</a></div>

<h3><span id=".E4.BB.BB.E6.84.8F.E9.A1.B9.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="任意项级数_2">任意项级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="编辑章节：任意项级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span id=".E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E9.A1.B9.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="函数项级数">函数项级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="编辑章节：函数项级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E5.9F.9F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="收敛域">收敛域</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="编辑章节：收敛域">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>对区间<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {I}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">I</mi>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

<h3><span id=".E4.B8.80.E8.87.B4.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="一致收敛">一致收敛</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="编辑章节：一致收敛">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E6%94%B6%E6%95%9B" title="一致收敛">一致收敛</a></div>
<p>函数项级数的取值可以在它的收敛域上用和函数定义，但和函数的性质可能会和级数的每一项不同。比如说，当函数项级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∑<!-- ∑ --></mo>
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\sum u_{n}(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a10b7acc5f2f8a6a31495264b92f4656c2fbef66" style="vertical-align: -1.338ex; width:9.429ex; height:3.843ex;"/></span>中的每一项<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle u_{n}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mi>u</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>n</mi>
</mrow>
</msub>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle u_{n}(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="u_{n}(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2704549d2546099f2638838b0767e7a07fa5c7fa" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.687ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>在收敛域上都是<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="连续函数">连续函数</a>时，和函数未必会是连续函数。以下是一个例子：
</p>

<p>然而，如果函数项级数能够满足某些更严格的条件的话，可以证明级数的和函数的规则性将会等于每一项函数的规则性，这就是所谓的<b><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E6%94%B6%E6%95%9B" title="一致收敛">一致收敛</a></b>性质。和<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97" title="序列">函数列</a>的一致收敛性质一样，函数项级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum u_{n}(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mrow>

<mi>x</mi>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">I</mi>

</math></span><img alt="S_{n}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9f049ac28d4ac8097b625f9d71c1f22b2ebd1bc4" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.643ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span> 在区间<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {I}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\rightarrow \infty }\left\|S-S_{n}\right\|_{\mathcal {I}}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<dd>或者写成<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \lim _{n\rightarrow \infty }\left\|\sum _{k=n}^{\infty }u_{k}\right\|_{\mathcal {I}}=0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E7.BB.9D.E5.AF.B9.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="绝对收敛_2">绝对收敛</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="编辑章节：绝对收敛">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>函数项级数也有绝对收敛的概念。对于某个给定的区间<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {I}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</p><p>绝对收敛的（连续？）函数在每一点都收敛，并且在区间<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {I}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.B9.82.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="幂级数_2">幂级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="编辑章节：幂级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%82%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="幂级数">幂级数</a></div>
<p>形同<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum a_{n}(x-x_{0})^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<h4><span id=".E5.B9.82.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E6.94.B6.E6.95.9B.E5.9F.9F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="幂函数的收敛域">幂函数的收敛域</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="编辑章节：幂函数的收敛域">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>根据<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="阿贝尔定理">阿贝尔定理</a>，它的收敛域是一个关于零对称的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8C%BA%E9%97%B4" title="区间">区间</a>，即为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (-R,R)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>R</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>R</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (-R,R)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="(-R,R)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/264e0f899423ec172f1d44168fd42644b826f591" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.179ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>（可开可闭）的形式。这个正数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>（可以是无穷大）叫做幂级数的<b>收敛半径</b>。并有定理：
</p><p>设幂级数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \sum a_{n}x^{n}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="R=0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b7e38203eea12f5613721e2fc5e185b8eef9e800" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.025ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E5.B9.82.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.92.8C.E5.87.BD.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="幂级数的和函数">幂级数的和函数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="编辑章节：幂级数的和函数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>求解幂级数的和函数有时需要利用先对各项积分（或求导）以得到一个方便利用已有公式进行求和的形式，在求和后在对各项求导（或积分）。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.B8.90.E8.BF.9B.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="渐进级数">渐进级数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="编辑章节：渐进级数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><b>渐进级数</b>是用来对某些函数的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%97%B4%E6%96%AD%E7%82%B9" title="间断点">间断点</a>附近的情况进行逼近的级数。渐进级数一般是发散的，它的部分和趋于无穷大，因此可以很好地逼近一个趋于无穷大的函数。但要注意的是，渐进级数提供的逼近是相对的，即只是比值趋于一致，与函数值之间的误差并不像收敛的级数一样趋于无穷小。一般来说，渐进级数在若干项后便达到最小的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%AF%E5%B7%AE" title="绝对误差">绝对误差</a>，之后的绝对误差一般会增大甚至趋于无穷。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.91.E6.95.A3.E7.BA.A7.E6.95.B0.E7.9A.84.E5.92.8C"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="发散级数的和">发散级数的和</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="编辑章节：发散级数的和">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%91%E6%95%A3%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0" title="发散级数">发散级数</a></div>
<p>发散级数的部分和没有极限，但是在应用中可以使用比较弱的级数和定义，比如<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%87%E8%90%A8%E7%BD%97%E6%B1%82%E5%92%8C" title="切萨罗求和">切萨罗求和</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E6%B1%82%E5%92%8C" title="阿贝尔求和">阿贝尔求和</a>以及<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E6%B1%82%E5%92%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="欧拉求和（页面不存在）">欧拉求和</a>。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.8E.A8.E5.B9.BF"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="推广">推广</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="编辑章节：推广">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>级数的概念可以在任何的<a href="/wiki/%E9%98%BF%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E7%BE%A4" title="阿贝尔群">对称</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%93%E6%89%91%E7%BE%A4" title="拓扑群">拓扑群</a>中定义，常用的是在一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%B4%E6%8B%BF%E8%B5%AB%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="巴拿赫空间">巴拿赫空间</a>（比如实数或复数空间）中。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.A7.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参见">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BA%A7%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="编辑章节：参见">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
